$CATEGORY: $course$ / Examples / For_Loops_Printing1

::For Loops Level 1 #000::
What is the following output of the code?
<pre>for (int d = 82; d > 42; d = d - 10)
\{
	cout << d << " ";
\}	{
	=82 72 62 52 
	~72 62 52 
	~72 62 52 42 
	~82 72 62 
	~82 72 62 52 42 
	}

::For Loops Level 1 #001::
What is the following output of the code?
<pre>for (int h = 3; h <= 7; h = h + 1)
\{
	cout << h << " ";
\}	{
	=3 4 5 6 7 
	~4 5 6 7 
	~4 5 6 7 8 
	~3 4 5 6 
	~3 4 5 6 7 8 
	}

::For Loops Level 3 #500::
How many times does the '*' print?
<pre>for (int i = 5; i >= 3; i = i - 1)
\{
	for (int j = 7; j < 10; j = j + 1)
	\{
		cout << '*' << " ";
	\}
\}</pre>	{
	=9
	~4
	~3
	~12
	~16
	}

	~20

	}

	=20
